- Third term: `3.629*epsilon^0.5976*T - 3.629*316.19*epsilon^0.5976` = `3.629*T*epsilon^0.5976 - 1147.5*epsilon^0.5976`

So GT = `-1.648*T*epsilon + 552.3*epsilon - 0.2255*T + 71.31 + 3.629*T*epsilon^0.5976 - 1147.5*epsilon^0.5976`

The GT has these basis functions:
1. `T*epsilon` (linear in both)
2. `epsilon` (linear)
3. `T` (linear)
4. Constant
5. `T*epsilon^0.5976` (T times fractional power of epsilon)
6. `epsilon^0.5976` (fractional power)

Key structural features: The GT depends on **both T and epsilon**, with a fractional power of epsilon (~0.6), and terms involving T multiplied by epsilon^0.6.

Now let me check each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** No T dependence at all. GT depends on T. Cannot match.
Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** Has `exp(c4/T)` and `exp(c2*epsilon)` - exponential terms. GT has no exponentials. Cannot zero out all T-dependent terms since GT needs T dependence.
Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** `T*c0*epsilon + c1*epsilon/(c2 + epsilon) + c3*exp(c4*sin(c5*epsilon + c6))`. Has T*epsilon but needs T alone and T*epsilon^0.6. Missing T term and the exp(sin(...)) can't produce epsilon^0.6 * T.
Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 4:** `T*c0*epsilon + T*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*epsilon) + c5*(c6 + Max(0, epsilon))^c7 + c8*epsilon*exp(c9/T)`
Has T*epsilon, T, constant, exp(epsilon), (epsilon)^c7, epsilon*exp(c9/T). 
GT needs T*epsilon^0.6 but this has no such term. The term `epsilon*exp(c9/T)` is not T*epsilon^0.6. The `(epsilon)^c7` term doesn't have T. Missing T*epsilon^0.6.
Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 5:** No T*epsilon^0.6 term. Has polynomial/rational terms in epsilon only plus T*epsilon.
Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 6:** Complex rational expressions. No T*epsilon^0.6 term.
Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 7:** `T*c0*epsilon + T*c1 + c2*exp(c3*Max(0,epsilon)) + c4 + c5*exp(c6*epsilon) + c7/(c8+Max(0,epsilon))^5`. No T*epsilon^0.6.
Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 8:** No T*epsilon^0.6 term.
Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 9:** `T*c0*epsilon + T*c1*log(c2*exp(c3*|epsilon| + c4/T) + 1) + c5*epsilon/(c6+epsilon) + c7*log(c8*exp(c9*epsilon)+1)`. The log-exp term could potentially simplify but not to T*epsilon^0.6.
Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 10-50:** Let me scan for candidates that have both `T*epsilon` and `T*epsilon^c` (fractional power with T).

Looking through all candidates, I need `T*epsilon^0.6` type terms. Let me check:

- **Candidate 11:** Has `c7*exp(c8/T)*Max(0,epsilon)^c9` - this gives `exp(c8/T)*epsilon^c9`, not `T*epsilon^c9`.
- **Candidate 25:** Has `exp(c6/T)*sin(...)` - not T*epsilon^0.6.
- **Candidate 34:** Has `epsilon^c5*exp(c6*epsilon)*log(T*c7+1)` - log(T) not T.

- **Candidate 28:** `epsilon^c5*log(T*c6+1)` - log(T) not T.

None of the candidates contain a `T*epsilon^(fractional power)` term, which is essential for the GT.
